## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical kinetics
**Analysis**: This task belongs to the field of chemical kinetics, where we study the rates of chemical reactions and their concentration-time dependence. The rate of change of concentration (dA_dt) is likely to be related to the concentration (A) and time (t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zeroth-order kinetics: Rate = c0 (constant reaction rate independent of reactant concentration)
- First-order kinetics: Rate = c0 * A (reaction rate linearly dependent on reactant concentration)
- Second-order kinetics: Rate = c0 * A^2 (reaction rate quadratically dependent on reactant concentration)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation, adapt to kinetics context: Rate = c0 * A / (A + c1))
- Haldane kinetics: Rate = c0 * A / (A + c1 * K) (considering both substrate and product inhibition)
- Prout-Tompkins equation: dA_dt = c0 * (A + c1)^c2 (describing autocatalytic reactions)
- Power-law kinetics: Rate = c0 * A^c1 (empirical representation of reaction rates)
- Birch-Monod equation: Rate = c0 * A / (A + c1)^c2 (representing cooperative binding of reactants)
- Monod kinetics: Rate = c0 * A / (A + c1 + c2 * A^2) (including substrate inhibition)
- Generalized rate equation: Rate = c0 * A^c1 * exp(c2 / T) (considering temperature dependence)
- Monod-Huffmann model: dA_dt = c0 * A / (A + c1)^c2 * exp(c3 / T) (accounting for temperature effects)
- Automodel: dA_dt = c0 * A^c1 * exp(c2 / (t + c3)) (introducing time-dependent rate coefficient)

- (1) rate = c0*A^c1 
- (2) rate = c0/(c1+A) 
- (3) rate = c0*A/(A+c1) 
- (4) rate = c0*A/(A+c1*c2) 
- (5) rate = c0*c1^c2/(1+c1^c2*A) 
- (6) rate = c0*A^c1/(c2+A^c1) 
- (7) rate = c0*A/(c1+A^c2) 
- (8) rate = c0*A/(A+c1*A^c2) 
- (9) rate = c0*A/(c1+A+c2*A^c2) 
- (10) rate = c0*c1^c2/(1+c1^c2/A)

- (14) rate = c0*c1^c2/(A+c1^c2*A^c3)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Growth/decay in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ exp(c*t), exp(c*A), exp(-c*A)
- Sigmoidal (logistic) behavior in reaction rates ŌåÆ 1/(1+c*x), 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), 1/(1+exp(c*x))
- Scaling laws in reaction rates ŌåÆ Power-law relations (c0 * A^c1, c0 * A^c1 * t^c2)
- Coupling between reactant and time in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Multiplicative interactions (c0 * A * t, c0 * A^c1 * t^c2)
- Autocatalysis in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Positive feedback loops (c0 * A * (A + c1)^c2, c0 * (A + c1)^c2)
- Substrate inhibition in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Competitive interactions (c0 * A / (A + c1), c0 * A / (A + c1)^c2)
- Cooperative binding in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Cooperative effects (c0 * A / (A + c1)^c2, c0 * A / (A + c1 + c2 * A^2))
- Catalysis in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Enzyme effects (c0 * A / (A + c1), c0 * S / (S + c1))
- Temperature dependence in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Arrhenius expression (c0 * exp(c1 / T), c0 * exp(c1 / (t + c2)))
- Catalyst inhibition in chemical reaction rates ŌåÆ Negative feedback loops (c0 * A / (A + c1)^c2, c0 * (A + c1)^c2)
